                \begin{minipage}{\textwidth}
                \item $\ex x \ [(Fx \ta Gx) \ra Hx] : \all x \ [(Fx \ta Gx) \ra Ha]$ \\
                    Invalid.
                    \vspace{1em}\\
\begin{tikzpicture}[every text node part/.style={align=center}]
    \node (1) at (0,-1) {$\ex x \ [(Fx \ta Gx) \ra Hx]$};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]1.center) {1.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]1.center) {Premise.};

    \node (2) at (0,-2) {$\s \all x \ [(Fx \ta Gx) \ra Ha]$};
    \draw (1) -- (2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]2.center) {2.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]2.center) {Negated conclusion.};

    \node (3) at (0,-3) {$\ex x \ [\s ((Fx \ta Gx) \ra Ha)]$};
    \draw (2) -- (3);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]3.center) {3.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]3.center) {2 quantifier-equivalence.};

    \node (4) at (0,-4) {$\s ((Fb \ta Gb) \ra Ha)$};
    \draw (3) -- (4);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]4.center) {4.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]4.center) {3 EIN.};

    \node (5) at (0,-5) {$Fb \ta Gb$};
    \draw (4) -- (5);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]5.center) {5.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]5.center) {From line 4.};

    \node (6) at (0,-6) {$\s Ha$};
    \draw (5) -- (6);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]6.center) {6.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]6.center) {From line 5.};

    \node (7) at (0,-7) {$Fb$};
    \draw (6) -- (7);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]7.center) {7.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]7.center) {From line 5.};

    \node (8) at (0,-8) {$Gb$};
    \draw (7) -- (8);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]8.center) {8.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]8.center) {From line 5.};

    \node (9) at (0,-9) {$(Fc \ta Gc) \ra Hc$};
    \draw (8) -- (9);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]9.center) {9.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]9.center) {1 EIN.};

    \node (10-1) at (-1,-10) {$\s (Fc \ta Gc)$};
    \draw (9) -- (10-1);
    \node (10-2) at (+1,-10) {$Hc$ \\ \cmark};
    \draw (9) -- (10-2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]10.center) {10.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]10.center) {From line 9.};

    \node (11-1-1) at (-1,-11) {$\s Fc$ \\ \cmark};
    \draw (10-1) -- (11-1-1);
    \node (11-1-2) at (+0,-11) {$\s Gc$ \\ \cmark};
    \draw (10-1) -- (11-1-2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]1.center |- 11-1-1) {11.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]1.center |- 11-1-1) {From line 10.};
\end{tikzpicture}
                    \vspace{1em}
                \end{minipage}
                \begin{minipage}{\textwidth}
                \item $: \ex x \ [Fx \ta Gx] \ra (\ex x \ [Fx] \ta \ex x \ [Gx])$ \\
                    Valid.
                    \vspace{1em}\\
\begin{tikzpicture}[every text node part/.style={align=center}]
    \node (1) at (0,-1) {$\s (\ex x \ [Fx \ta Gx] \ra (\ex x \ [Fx] \ta \ex x \ [Gx]))$};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]1.center) {1.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]1.center) {Negated conclusion.};

    \node (2) at (0,-2) {$\ex x \ [Fx \ta Gx]$};
    \draw (1) -- (2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]2.center) {2.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]2.center) {From line 1.};

    \node (3) at (0,-3) {$\s (\ex x \ [Fx] \ta \ex x \ [Gx])$};
    \draw (2) -- (3);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]3.center) {3.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]3.center) {From line 1.};

    \node (4) at (0,-4) {$Fa \ta Ga$};
    \draw (3) -- (4);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]4.center) {4.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]4.center) {2 EIN.};

    \node (5) at (0,-5) {$Fa$};
    \draw (4) -- (5);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]5.center) {5.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]5.center) {From line 4.};

    \node (6) at (0,-6) {$Ga$};
    \draw (5) -- (6);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]6.center) {6.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]6.center) {From line 4.};

    \node (7-1) at (-1,-7) {$\s \ex x \ [Fx]$};
    \draw (6) -- (7-1);
    \node (7-2) at (+1,-7) {$\s \ex x \ [Gx]$};
    \draw (6) -- (7-2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]7.center) {7.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]7.center) {From line 3.};

    \node (8-1) at (-1,-8) {$\all x \ [\s Fx]$};
    \draw (7-1) -- (8-1);
    \node (8-2) at (+1,-8) {$\all x \ [\s Gx]$};
    \draw (7-2) -- (8-2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]8.center) {8.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]8.center) {7 quantifier-equivalence.};

    \node (9-1) at (-1,-9) {$\s Fa$ \\ \xmark 5, 9};
    \draw (8-1) -- (9-1);
    \node (9-2) at (+1,-9) {$\s Ga$ \\ \xmark 5, 6};
    \draw (8-2) -- (9-2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]9.center) {9.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]9.center) {8 UIN.};
\end{tikzpicture}
                    \vspace{1em}
                \end{minipage}
            \end{enumerate}
    \end{enumerate}

    \subsection*{EXERCISE 7.2}

    \begin{enumerate}[label=\arabic*,leftmargin=*]
        \item The consistency-trees are the followings.\\
            When an IQLI is specified, the domain is the whole numbers.
            \nopagebreak
            \begin{enumerate}[label=\arabic*.]
                \begin{minipage}{\textwidth}
                \item $\ex x \ [Fx] : \all x \ [Fx]$ \\
                    Invalid. IQLI: $F$: \{1\}, $a$: 1, $b$: 2.
                    \vspace{1em}\\
\begin{tikzpicture}[every text node part/.style={align=center}]
    \node (1) at (0,-1) {$\ex x \ [Fx]$};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]1.center) {1.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]1.center) {Premise.};

    \node (2) at (0,-2) {$\s \all x \ [Fx]$};
    \draw (1) -- (2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]2.center) {2.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]2.center) {Negated conclusion.};

    \node (3) at (0,-3) {$\ex x \ [\s Fx]$};
    \draw (2) -- (3);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]3.center) {3.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]3.center) {2 quantifier-equivalence.};

    \node (4) at (0,-4) {$Fa$};
    \draw (3) -- (4);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]4.center) {4.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]4.center) {1 EIN.};

    \node (5) at (0,-5) {$\s Fb$ \\ \cmark};
    \draw (4) -- (5);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-3.0cm]5.center) {5.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+3.0cm]5.center) {3 EIN.};
\end{tikzpicture}
                    \vspace{1em}
                \end{minipage}
                \begin{minipage}{\textwidth}
                \item $\all x \ [\s Fx] : \s \ex x \ [Fx]$ \\
                    Valid.
                    \vspace{1em}\\
\begin{tikzpicture}[every text node part/.style={align=center}]
    \node (1) at (0,-1) {$\all x \ [\s Fx]$};

                \end{minipage}
                \begin{minipage}{\textwidth}
                \item $\ex x \ [Fx \tv Gx], \ex x \ [\s Fx] : \ex x \ [Gx]$ \\

                \begin{minipage}{\textwidth}
                \item $: (\ex x \ [Fx] \ta \ex x \ [Gx]) \ra (\ex x \ [Fx \ta Gx])$ \\

    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]10.center) {10.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]10.center) {6 UIN.};

    \node (11-1) at (-1,-11) {$\s Fa$ \\ \xmark \ 7, 11};
    \draw (10) -- (11-1);
    \node (11-2) at (+1,-11) {$\s Ga$};
    \draw (10) -- (11-2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]1.center |- 11-1) {11.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]1.center |- 11-1) {From line 9.};

    \node (12-1) at (0,-12) {$\s Fb$ \\ \cmark};
    \draw (11-2) -- (12-1);
    \node (12-2) at (+2,-12) {$\s Gb$ \\ \xmark \ 8, 12};
    \draw (11-2) -- (12-2);
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=-5.0cm]1.center |- 12-1) {12.};
    \node[anchor=west] at ([xshift=+5.0cm]1.center |- 12-1) {From line 10.};
\end{tikzpicture}
                    \vspace{1em}
                \end{minipage}
            \end{enumerate}
    \end{enumerate}
\end{document}
